Exam Modules:
Features:
AI-Generated Practice Papers: System generates unique timed papers matching the exact format of each exam (number of questions, marks distribution, negative marking rules)
Competition Simulation Mode: Full-screen timed test with exam conditions (no hints, no AI help, timer countdown, auto-submit on time expiry)
Detailed Post-Test Analysis: Per-question analysis showing: correct answer, student's answer, time spent, concept tag, difficulty level, recommended topics for improvement
Percentile Ranking: Student's score compared to other BabySteps students who attempted the same paper (anonymised)
Database Table: exam_attempts
Acceptance Criteria:
• AC1: AI-generated papers match official exam format (verified by subject experts)
• AC2: Competition simulation mode blocks all AI assistance, navigation away, and hints
• AC3: Percentile computed within 5 minutes of submission
• AC4: Post-test analysis loads within 3 seconds
• AC5: JEE/NEET foundation content reviewed by coaching industry experts
6.4 MODULE: EDGE AI AT SCALE (EDG)
BS-EDG-001-F | Optimised On-Device Model Routing
This requirement SHALL enforce strict tenant isolation, security-by-default configuration, and operational resilience. All enterprise-grade decisions SHALL be auditable, versioned, and compliant with applicable regulations. Failure handling, disaster recovery, and graceful degradation SHALL be explicitly supported. Observability SHALL cover SLAs, SLOs, and compliance metrics. No cross-tenant data access SHALL be possible under any condition.
Priority: P0
Description: Intelligent routing system decides whether a query is served by the on-device model (edge) or sent to the cloud, optimising for cost, latency, and quality.
Routing Decision Matrix:
Routing Algorithm:
function routeQuery(query, student, connectivity):
complexity = classifyComplexity(query)  // Fast rule-based classifier
if connectivity == 'offline':
return 'edge'  // Always edge when offline
if complexity == 'low':
return 'edge'  // Save cloud cost
if complexity == 'medium' AND student.iq_level <= 2:
return 'edge'  // Phi-3 handles well for L1/L2 students
if complexity == 'medium' AND student.iq_level == 3:
return 'cloud'  // L3 students need deeper responses
if complexity == 'high':
return 'cloud'  // Always cloud for complex tasks
return 'cloud'  // Default
Cost Projections at Scale:
Target: < ₹50/student/month AI inference cost at 1M students.
Database Table: inference_routing_log
Acceptance Criteria:
• AC1: 60–70% of queries routed to edge (measured over 30-day window)
• AC2: AI inference cost < ₹50/student/month at 1M scale
• AC3: Edge response latency < 1 second; cloud < 5 seconds
• AC4: Quality of edge responses evaluated monthly (sample 1,000 queries, compare to cloud equivalent)
• AC5: Routing decision adds < 50ms overhead
BS-EDG-002-F | Gemma 2B On-Device for Ultra-Low-End Tablets
This requirement SHALL enforce strict tenant isolation, security-by-default configuration, and operational resilience. All enterprise-grade decisions SHALL be auditable, versioned, and compliant with applicable regulations. Failure handling, disaster recovery, and graceful degradation SHALL be explicitly supported. Observability SHALL cover SLAs, SLOs, and compliance metrics. No cross-tenant data access SHALL be possible under any condition.
Priority: P1
Description: For devices with < 3GB RAM where Phi-3 Mini cannot run, deploy Gemma 2B (1.5GB on-device footprint) as a lighter alternative.
Capability Comparison:
Auto-Detection:
• On first launch, app runs device benchmark
• If RAM < 3GB → download Gemma 2B model
• If RAM ≥ 3GB → download Phi-3 Mini
• Parent informed: "We're downloading a [X GB] AI assistant optimised for this device."
Acceptance Criteria:
• AC1: Gemma 2B runs on Redmi A2 (2GB RAM) without crashes
• AC2: Device benchmark completes within 10 seconds and correctly selects model
• AC3: Gemma 2B handles simple Q&A at ≥ 85% quality compared to cloud (validated on 500-query test set)
• AC4: Model selection is transparent to parent ("AI optimised for your device")

BS-ADV-004-F | Peer Teaching Mode
This requirement SHALL enforce strict tenant isolation, security-by-default configuration, and operational resilience. All enterprise-grade decisions SHALL be auditable, versioned, and compliant with applicable regulations. Failure handling, disaster recovery, and graceful degradation SHALL be explicitly supported. Observability SHALL cover SLAs, SLOs, and compliance metrics. No cross-tenant data access SHALL be possible under any condition.
Priority: P1
Description: Students who achieve 5 stars on a concept can unlock "Teacher Mode" where they explain the concept to an AI student persona. The AI evaluates their teaching quality.
Flow:
Student earns 5★ on a concept → "Teacher Mode Unlocked! 🎓" notification
Student opens Teacher Mode → AI persona appears as a "younger student" character
AI persona asks: "Can you teach me about [Concept]? I'm having trouble understanding it."
Student explains via voice/text (3–5 minutes)
AI persona asks clarifying questions (simulating a confused student): "Wait, so does that mean...?" "Can you give me an example?"
Student responds to 2–3 follow-up questions
AI evaluates teaching quality:
◦ Accuracy of explanation
◦ Clarity and simplicity
◦ Use of examples
◦ Patience with follow-up questions
◦ Encouragement of the "learner"
Teaching star rating awarded (separate from learning stars)
Badge: "Great Teacher" earned after 5 successful teaching sessions
Database Table: peer_teaching_sessions
Acceptance Criteria:
• AC1: Teacher Mode unlocks ONLY for concepts with 5★ (server-enforced)
• AC2: AI persona asks genuinely probing questions (not generic)
• AC3: Teaching quality evaluation is separate from learning stars
• AC4: Parent can view child's teaching sessions and scores
• AC5: "Great Teacher" badge awarded after 5 sessions with teaching_star_rating ≥ 4
BS-ADV-005-F | AI-Moderated Study Groups
This requirement SHALL enforce strict tenant isolation, security-by-default configuration, and operational resilience. All enterprise-grade decisions SHALL be auditable, versioned, and compliant with applicable regulations. Failure handling, disaster recovery, and graceful degradation SHALL be explicitly supported. Observability SHALL cover SLAs, SLOs, and compliance metrics. No cross-tenant data access SHALL be possible under any condition.
Priority: P2
Description: Students in the same grade and tenant can join small study groups (3–5 students) for collaborative learning with AI moderation.
Structure:
• Groups formed by: Same grade + same current subject focus + similar IQ level (±1 level)
• Maximum 5 students per group
• AI moderator manages turn-taking, ensures participation, mediates disagreements
• Activities: Collaborative problem-solving, concept discussions, quiz competitions within group
• All text/voice communication screened by AI safety pipeline (BS-AIE-004-F) BEFORE delivery
Safety Rules:
• No free-text chat for ages < 10 (pre-defined response bubbles only)
• Ages 10+: Text chat with real-time AI screening (profanity, bullying, PII detection)
• No video between students (only text/voice)
• Parent opt-in required (OFF by default in parental controls)
• Any flagged content → session paused → mentor alerted
Acceptance Criteria:
• AC1: All student messages screened by AI before delivery to other students (no bypass)
• AC2: Parent opt-in required and is OFF by default
• AC3: Ages < 10 can only use pre-defined response bubbles
• AC4: Flagged content triggers immediate session pause and mentor alert within 5 minutes
• AC5: Group formation algorithm balances grade, subject, and IQ level

Appendix C: Phase 1 Content Requirements
Each concept requires: name, description, learning objectives, CBSE standard code, prerequisite links, RAG source text, 28+ questions (10 easy, 10 medium, 5 hard, 3 expert), optional illustrations.
Content Creation Timeline:
• Month 1: Math Grades 1–2 (50 concepts) + English Grades 1–2 (20 concepts) = 70 concepts
• Month 2: Math Grades 3–4 (40 concepts) + English Grades 3–5 (30 concepts) + Hindi (15 concepts) = 85 concepts
• Month 3: Math Grade 5 (30 concepts) + Hindi (15 concepts) + QA and review = 45 concepts + all review
Appendix D: Glossary
*End of Document — Version 2.0 (Complete)*
*All four phases (Phase 1 through Phase 4) are fully specified in this document.*
*No further FSD supplements required. Implementation begins with Phase 1 Sprint 1.*
Technology Stack Mandate:All backend services SHALL be implemented in Python. All frontend user interfaces SHALL be implemented in React. Node.js SHALL be used for build tooling, orchestration, and supporting services only. No alternative primary languages or frameworks are permitted unless explicitly approved.
